in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec3 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat10_1.xy = texture2D(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xz;
    u_xlat16_35 = u_xlat10_1.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_35 = _Mask * u_xlat16_35 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_35 + (-_Cutoff);
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat16_3.x<0.0;
    if(u_xlatb1){discard;}
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-_colorSkin.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + _colorSkin.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_36 = u_xlat10_0.w * u_xlat10_0.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_36 = max(u_xlat16_36, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat10_1.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_15.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = max(u_xlat33, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat7.xy).x;
    u_xlatb34 = u_xlat34<u_xlat7.z;
    u_xlat7.x = (u_xlatb34) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat8.xy).x;
    u_xlatb34 = u_xlat34<u_xlat8.z;
    u_xlat7.y = (u_xlatb34) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat8.xy).x;
    u_xlatb34 = u_xlat34<u_xlat8.z;
    u_xlat7.z = (u_xlatb34) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    u_xlat34 = texture2D(_MainLightShadowmapTexture, u_xlat8.xy).x;
    u_xlatb34 = u_xlat34<u_xlat8.z;
    u_xlat7.w = (u_xlatb34) ? 0.0 : 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat7, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_26 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_15.x = u_xlat16_15.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_26;
    u_xlatb34 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
    u_xlatb39 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
    u_xlatb34 = u_xlatb34 || u_xlatb39;
    u_xlat16_15.x = (u_xlatb34) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_15.x;
    u_xlat16_26 = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_36;
    u_xlat34 = u_xlat16_26 * u_xlat16_26;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat33) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = inversesqrt(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat33) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat33 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
    u_xlat33 = clamp(u_xlat33, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_37 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_37 = abs(u_xlat16_37) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_37 = min(u_xlat16_37, 1.0);
    u_xlat39 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat39 = clamp(u_xlat39, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x + u_xlat16_5.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * (-u_xlat16_5.xxx) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat16_37) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat16_38;
    u_xlat16_9.x = (-u_xlat16_36) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_36 * u_xlat16_9.x;
    u_xlat16_9.x = u_xlat16_9.x * 6.0;
    u_xlat10_8 = textureCube(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_9.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat10_8.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_5.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_5.x = max(u_xlat16_5.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_5.x = log2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_5.x = exp2(u_xlat16_5.x);
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_5.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat10_8.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xxx;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_26 * u_xlat16_26 + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat18 = (-u_xlat16_36) + 1.0;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_38 * u_xlat18 + 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat33);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + _ShadowOffset;
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat29 = (-u_xlat39) * u_xlat39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat40 = u_xlat16_26 * u_xlat39;
    u_xlat29 = u_xlat40 * u_xlat40 + u_xlat29;
    u_xlat29 = u_xlat16_26 / u_xlat29;
    u_xlat29 = u_xlat29 * u_xlat29;

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat16_3.x<0.0;
    if(u_xlatb1){discard;}

    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat10_1.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + _colorSkin.xyz;

    u_xlat16_36 = min(u_xlat16_36, 1.0);

    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_15.xyz;
    u_xlat16_15.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_15.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_15.x);

vec3 u_xlat5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
float u_xlat9;
float u_xlat21;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2DShadow hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(4) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(5) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD7;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
vec3 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_3;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_6;
vec3 u_xlat7;
vec3 u_xlat8;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_9;
float u_xlat10;
bool u_xlatb10;
mediump float u_xlat16_11;
float u_xlat20;
mediump float u_xlat16_21;
float u_xlat30;
mediump float u_xlat16_31;
float u_xlat32;
mediump float u_xlat16_33;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xy = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_0.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11 * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _Mask * u_xlat16_1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_1.x + (-_Cutoff);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_21<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_21<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset0.xyz;
    vec3 txVec0 = vec3(u_xlat0.xy,u_xlat0.z);
    u_xlat0.x = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec0, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset1.xyz;
    vec3 txVec1 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat0.y = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec1, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset2.xyz;
    vec3 txVec2 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat0.z = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec2, 0.0);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD7.xyz + _MainLightShadowOffset3.xyz;
    vec3 txVec3 = vec3(u_xlat2.xy,u_xlat2.z);
    u_xlat0.w = textureLod(hlslcc_zcmp_MainLightShadowmapTexture, txVec3, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_1.x = dot(u_xlat0, vec4(0.25, 0.25, 0.25, 0.25));
    u_xlat16_21 = (-_MainLightShadowParams.x) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * _MainLightShadowParams.x + u_xlat16_21;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = 0.0>=vs_TEXCOORD7.z;
#endif
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb10 = !!(vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0);
#else
    u_xlatb10 = vs_TEXCOORD7.z>=1.0;
#endif
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlatb10 || u_xlatb0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = (u_xlatb0) ? 1.0 : u_xlat16_1.x;
    u_xlat16_21 = _faceshadowScale * 0.400000006 + u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_21 = min(max(u_xlat16_21, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = min(u_xlat16_3.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyw = u_xlat16_4.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_4.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyw;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat10 = log2(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat10 = exp2(u_xlat10);
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10 = min(max(u_xlat10, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat10 = clamp(u_xlat10, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(u_xlat10);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = max(u_xlat16_3.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = max(u_xlat16_5.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_6.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_6.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_6.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat10 = dot(u_xlat16_6.xyz, u_xlat16_6.xyz);
    u_xlat10 = max(u_xlat10, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat10 = inversesqrt(u_xlat10);
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * vec3(u_xlat10) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat10) * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat10 = dot(u_xlat2.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
    u_xlat10 = inversesqrt(u_xlat10);
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat10) * u_xlat2.xyz;
    u_xlat10 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat10 = min(max(u_xlat10, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat10 = clamp(u_xlat10, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat20 = (-u_xlat10) * u_xlat10 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_2.w * u_xlat16_2.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_21 = max(u_xlat16_21, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_21 = min(u_xlat16_21, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_21 * u_xlat16_21;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10 + u_xlat20;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat16_31 / u_xlat10;
    u_xlat20 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_31 + 1.0;
    u_xlat20 = float(1.0) / u_xlat20;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat10;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat16_21 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat10 = u_xlat10 * u_xlat32;
    u_xlat10 = min(u_xlat10, 100.0);
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat10 * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat8.xyz = u_xlat8.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-_colorSkin.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_0.www * u_xlat16_6.xyz + _colorSkin.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_5.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot((-u_xlat7.xyz), u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_31 + u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_4.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_31)) + (-u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = abs(u_xlat16_31) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_31 = min(u_xlat16_31, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = (-u_xlat16_21) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_21 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_5.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_33 = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_33 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_33 = max(u_xlat16_33, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_33 = log2(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_33 = exp2(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat16_33);
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat20) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat30 * u_xlat30;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_21) + 1.0;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat16_21 + 1.0;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat32 * u_xlat32;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat30 + 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);

    u_xlat16_31 = (-u_xlat16_31) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat30 * u_xlat30;
    u_xlat16_33 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat16_33;
    u_xlat30 = (-u_xlat16_21) + 1.0;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat16_21 + 1.0;
    u_xlat32 = u_xlat32 * u_xlat32;
    u_xlat30 = u_xlat16_33 * u_xlat30 + 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat30) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_21);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_21 = dot(u_xlat16_4.xyz, u_xlat16_9.xyz);
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_21) * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = max(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = min(u_xlat16_9.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat16_9.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat32 * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_21 = (-u_xlat32) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_21 + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_31 / u_xlat16_21;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_31);
    u_xlat16_9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_31) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_31 = dot(u_xlat16_9.xyz, u_xlat16_4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_31 = clamp(u_xlat16_31, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 * u_xlat16_31 + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_31 = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_31 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_31 * u_xlat16_21;
    u_xlat16_21 = clamp(u_xlat16_21, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_31 = u_xlat16_21 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 * u_xlat16_21;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_21 * u_xlat16_31;
    u_xlat16_31 = (-_RimlightShadowScale) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_31 + _RimlightShadowScale;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_1.x * u_xlat16_21;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_6.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_4.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_6.xyz + u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xxx * u_xlat16_4.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = max(u_xlat16_1.xzw, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = min(u_xlat16_1.xzw, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw + u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_11) * u_xlat10_2.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    SV_Target0.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    return;
}

void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat9 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat21 = u_xlat21 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat21 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat9 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat3.xyz = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat21 = dot(u_xlat3.xyz, u_xlat3.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = max(u_xlat21, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat21 = inversesqrt(u_xlat21);
    u_xlat3.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat3.xyz;
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat5.xyz = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat5.xyz);
    u_xlat21 = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = vec3(u_xlat21) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    vs_TEXCOORD7 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4_MainLightWorldToShadow[3];
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_6.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_6.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_6.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

{
    u_xlat16_0.xy = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_0.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_11 = u_xlat16_11 * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _Mask * u_xlat16_1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_21 = u_xlat16_1.x + (-_Cutoff);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_21<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_21<0.0;

    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;

mediump vec3 u_xlat16_16;
float u_xlat19;
float u_xlat24;
int u_xlati24;
bool u_xlatb24;
mediump float u_xlat16_28;
float u_xlat31;
float u_xlat36;
bool u_xlatb36;
float u_xlat37;
mediump float u_xlat16_38;
mediump float u_xlat16_39;
mediump float u_xlat16_40;
mediump float u_xlat16_41;
float u_xlat42;
float u_xlat43;
mediump float u_xlat16_44;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xz;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_1.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = _Mask * u_xlat16_38 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_38 + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(u_xlat16_3.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat16_3.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb1){discard;}
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-_colorSkin.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + _colorSkin.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_0.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_39 = max(u_xlat16_39, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_39 = min(u_xlat16_39, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_1.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = max(u_xlat36, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat37 = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_16.x;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat36 = min(max(u_xlat36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat36 = clamp(u_xlat36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat42 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_40 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_40)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_41 = (-u_xlat16_39) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_41;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_5.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_8.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_8.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_8.x = max(u_xlat16_8.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_8.x = log2(u_xlat16_8.x);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_8.x = exp2(u_xlat16_8.x);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xxx;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_16.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_39) + 1.0;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat19 + 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = log2(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat19 = exp2(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat19 = min(max(u_xlat19, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat19 = clamp(u_xlat19, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat31 = (-u_xlat42) * u_xlat42 + 1.0;
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat43 * u_xlat43 + u_xlat31;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat16_16.x / u_xlat31;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat31 * u_xlat31;
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat16_39 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat31 * u_xlat43;
    u_xlat31 = min(u_xlat31, 100.0);
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat31;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat31 * 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat31) * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_40 = _faceshadowScale * 0.400000006 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = max(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_40);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_10.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_44 = (-u_xlat1.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44 + u_xlat13;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat16_44;
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_44 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_44);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_44) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_44 = min(max(u_xlat16_44, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_44 = clamp(u_xlat16_44, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_10.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44 + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_44 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_10.x;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_40 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44;

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_38 = _Mask * u_xlat16_38 + 1.0;

    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    vs_TEXCOORD2.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in highp vec3 vs_TEXCOORD2;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec3 u_xlat0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_0;
uint u_xlatu0;
vec3 u_xlat1;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
bool u_xlatb1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;

bool u_xlatb36;

mediump float u_xlat16_39;

mediump float u_xlat16_44;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_1 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_1.xy = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xz;
    u_xlat16_38 = u_xlat16_1.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_38 = _Mask * u_xlat16_38 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_38 + (-_Cutoff);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb1 = !!(u_xlat16_3.x<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb1 = u_xlat16_3.x<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb1){discard;}
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = (-_colorSkin.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_1.www * u_xlat16_3.xyz + _colorSkin.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3.xyz = u_xlat16_0.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat16_39 = u_xlat16_0.w * u_xlat16_0.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_39 = max(u_xlat16_39, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_39 = min(u_xlat16_39, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_1.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_2.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_16.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_16.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_16.x);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat16_16.xxx;
    u_xlat16_5.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_5.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_5.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = max(u_xlat36, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat6.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_16.x = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_39;
    u_xlat37 = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_16.x;
    u_xlat7.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * vec3(u_xlat36) + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat7.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
    u_xlat36 = inversesqrt(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat7.xyz = vec3(u_xlat36) * u_xlat7.xyz;
    u_xlat36 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat36 = min(max(u_xlat36, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat36 = clamp(u_xlat36, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_28 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat16_28 = abs(u_xlat16_28) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_28 = min(u_xlat16_28, 1.0);
    u_xlat42 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat42 = min(max(u_xlat42, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat42 = clamp(u_xlat42, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat7.x = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat7.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat7.x = min(max(u_xlat7.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat7.x = clamp(u_xlat7.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_40 = dot((-u_xlat1.xyz), u_xlat16_2.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 + u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * (-vec3(u_xlat16_40)) + (-u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat1.x = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_41 = (-u_xlat16_39) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_39 * u_xlat16_41;
    u_xlat16_41 = u_xlat16_41 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_5 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_41);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_5.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_8.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_8.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_8.x = max(u_xlat16_8.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_8.x = log2(u_xlat16_8.x);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_8.x = exp2(u_xlat16_8.x);
    u_xlat16_8.x = u_xlat16_8.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * u_xlat16_8.xxx;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat16_16.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat1.xxx;
    u_xlat19 = (-u_xlat16_39) + 1.0;
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat19 + 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat1.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_3.xyz + u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat19 = log2(u_xlat36);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat19 = exp2(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat19 = u_xlat19 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat19 = min(max(u_xlat19, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat19 = clamp(u_xlat19, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat31 = (-u_xlat42) * u_xlat42 + 1.0;
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat16_16.x * u_xlat42;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat43 * u_xlat43 + u_xlat31;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat16_16.x / u_xlat31;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat31 * u_xlat31;
    u_xlat43 = u_xlat16_39 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat31 * u_xlat43;
    u_xlat31 = min(u_xlat31, 100.0);
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat36 * u_xlat31;
    u_xlat31 = u_xlat31 * 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat9.xyz = vec3(u_xlat31) * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat9.xyz * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_40 = _faceshadowScale * 0.400000006 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = min(u_xlat16_8.xyz, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat19) * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = max(u_xlat16_8.xyz, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz + u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_40 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_40);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = dot(u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_10.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_40 = (-u_xlat16_28) + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat16_39 + 1.0;
    u_xlat1.x = u_xlat1.x * u_xlat1.x;
    u_xlat13 = u_xlat1.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_44 = (-u_xlat1.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44 + u_xlat13;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 / u_xlat16_44;
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_44 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_44);
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_44) * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_44 = dot(u_xlat16_10.xyz, u_xlat16_2.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_44 = min(max(u_xlat16_44, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_44 = clamp(u_xlat16_44, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_10.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44 + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_44 = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_10.x;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_40 = min(max(u_xlat16_40, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_40 = clamp(u_xlat16_40, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_44 = u_xlat16_40 * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_40;
    u_xlat16_40 = u_xlat16_40 * u_xlat16_44;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_3.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = _RimlightColor.www * u_xlat16_11.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_40) * u_xlat16_10.xyz;
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = max(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_10.xyz = min(u_xlat16_10.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = u_xlat16_8.xyz + u_xlat16_10.xyz;

void main()
{
    u_xlat10_0 = texture2D(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat10_1 = texture2D(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat10_1.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);

    u_xlat16_3.x = u_xlat16_38 + (-_Cutoff);

    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_29;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_34;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xy = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_0.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_10 * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _Mask * u_xlat16_1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_1.x + (-_Cutoff);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_19<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_19<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _faceshadowScale * 0.400000006 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = min(u_xlat16_1.xzw, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xzw, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = u_xlat16_5.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyw;
    u_xlat16_29 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_29 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_29);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_29 = u_xlat16_6.w * u_xlat16_6.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_32 / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32 + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat18;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat18;
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * vec3(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = max(u_xlat16_1.xzw, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_colorSkin.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + _colorSkin.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xzw + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot((-u_xlat4.xyz), u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * (-u_xlat16_2.xxx) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = abs(u_xlat16_32) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_34 = (-u_xlat16_29) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_34 = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_34;
    u_xlat16_34 = u_xlat16_34 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_34);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.y;
    u_xlat16_2.x = exp2(u_xlat16_2.x);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * unity_SpecCube0_HDR.x;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat16_2.xxx;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat9.xxx * u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat27 = (-u_xlat16_32) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = (-u_xlat16_32) + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat27 * u_xlat27;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_11.x * u_xlat16_11.x;
    u_xlat27 = (-u_xlat16_29) + 1.0;
    u_xlat4.x = u_xlat16_29 + 1.0;
    u_xlat4.x = u_xlat4.x * u_xlat4.x;
    u_xlat27 = u_xlat16_11.x * u_xlat27 + 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vec3(u_xlat27) * u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD1.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat0.xyz + u_xlat16_1.xzw;
    u_xlat16_11.x = dot(_AddLightDir.xyz, _AddLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_11.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_11.x);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xxx * _AddLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_11.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_11.x = min(max(u_xlat16_11.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_11.x = clamp(u_xlat16_11.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_8.xyz = vs_TEXCOORD8.yyy * _AddlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xxx * u_xlat16_8.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_1.xzw * u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = max(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(0.0, 0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = min(u_xlat16_11.xyz, vec3(100.0, 100.0, 100.0));
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw + u_xlat16_11.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat4.x * 0.125;
    u_xlat16_11.x = (-u_xlat4.x) * 0.125 + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_11.x + u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x / u_xlat16_11.x;
    u_xlat16_11.x = dot(_RimLightDir.xyz, _RimLightDir.xyz);
    u_xlat16_11.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_11.x);
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_11.xxx * _RimLightDir.xyz;
    u_xlat16_11.x = dot(u_xlat16_11.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_11.x = min(max(u_xlat16_11.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_11.x = clamp(u_xlat16_11.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_11.x + (-_RimlightScale);
    u_xlat16_11.x = (-_RimlightScale) + _RimlightScale2;
    u_xlat16_11.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat16_11.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_11.x * u_xlat16_2.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_2.x = min(max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_2.x = clamp(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_11.x = u_xlat16_2.x * -2.0 + 3.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x * u_xlat16_11.x;
    u_xlat16_11.xyz = u_xlat16_7.xyz * _RimlightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = (-_RimlightColor.xyz) * u_xlat16_7.xyz + _RimlightColor.xyz;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHAb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBr;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBg;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHBb;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 unity_SHC;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
UNITY_BINDING(1) uniform UnityPerMaterial {
#endif
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _MainTex_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _HairMap_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM vec4 _BumpMapNr2_ST;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _RoughNessOffset;

	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump float _MatMask;
	UNITY_UNIFORM mediump vec4 _SHColorScale;
#if HLSLCC_ENABLE_UNIFORM_BUFFERS
};
#endif
in highp vec4 in_POSITION0;
in highp vec3 in_NORMAL0;
in highp vec4 in_TANGENT0;
in highp vec2 in_TEXCOORD0;
out highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD6;
out mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
vec4 u_xlat0;
vec4 u_xlat1;
vec4 u_xlat2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_2;
vec4 u_xlat3;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_4;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_5;
float u_xlat8;
float u_xlat18;
float u_xlat19;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _MainTex_ST.xy + _MainTex_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat1 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    vs_TEXCOORD0.zw = u_xlat1.xy;
    gl_Position = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat18 = max(u_xlat18, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat18 = inversesqrt(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat18) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat1.y * u_xlat1.y;
    u_xlat2.x = u_xlat1.y * 0.25;
    u_xlat8 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + u_xlat2.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * 0.125 + (-u_xlat2.x);
    u_xlat3.y = u_xlat18 + 0.125;
    u_xlat3.x = u_xlat8 + 0.125;
    u_xlat16_4.xy = max(u_xlat3.xy, vec2(0.0, 0.0));
    u_xlat16_4.xy = u_xlat16_4.xy * vec2(vec2(_SHScale, _SHScale));
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.yyyy * _SHBotColor;
    u_xlat16_2 = u_xlat16_4.xxxx * _SHTopColor + u_xlat16_2;
    vs_TEXCOORD1 = u_xlat16_2 * _SHColorScale;
    u_xlat2.xyw = (-u_xlat0.xyz) + _WorldSpaceCameraPos.xyz;
    u_xlat1.w = u_xlat2.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD3 = u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0.xzw = in_TANGENT0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_TANGENT0.xxx + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat0.xzw = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_TANGENT0.zzz + u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat19 = dot(u_xlat0.xzw, u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat19 = max(u_xlat19, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat19 = inversesqrt(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(u_xlat19);
    u_xlat3.w = u_xlat2.y;
    vs_TEXCOORD4 = u_xlat3;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.zxy * u_xlat3.yzx;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat1.yzx * u_xlat3.zxy + (-u_xlat0.xzw);
    u_xlat1.x = in_TANGENT0.w * unity_WorldTransformParams.w;
    u_xlat2.xyz = u_xlat0.xzw * u_xlat1.xxx;
    vs_TEXCOORD5 = u_xlat2;
    vs_TEXCOORD6 = vec4(0.0, 0.0, 0.0, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_4.x = log2(abs(u_xlat0.y));
    u_xlat16_5.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _MainlightAttenuation;
    u_xlat16_5.z = u_xlat16_4.x * _RimlightAttenuation;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.xz = exp2(u_xlat16_5.xz);
    u_xlat16_4.x = _AddlightLerp * 2.0 + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * 5.0 + u_xlat0.y;
    u_xlat16_4.x = u_xlat16_4.x * _AddlightAttenuation;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_4.x = min(max(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_4.x = clamp(u_xlat16_4.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    vs_TEXCOORD8.y = u_xlat16_4.x * u_xlat16_4.x;
    vs_TEXCOORD8.w = 1.0;
    return;
}

#endif

#endif
UNITY_LOCATION(0) uniform mediump samplerCube unity_SpecCube0;
UNITY_LOCATION(1) uniform mediump sampler2D _MainTex;
UNITY_LOCATION(2) uniform mediump sampler2D _BumpMapNr;
UNITY_LOCATION(3) uniform mediump sampler2D _MixMap;
in highp vec4 vs_TEXCOORD0;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD1;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD3;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD4;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD5;
in mediump vec4 vs_TEXCOORD8;
layout(location = 0) out mediump vec4 SV_Target0;
vec4 u_xlat0;
mediump vec2 u_xlat16_0;
bool u_xlatb0;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_1;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_2;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_3;
vec3 u_xlat4;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_5;
mediump vec4 u_xlat16_6;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_7;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_8;
vec3 u_xlat9;
mediump float u_xlat16_10;
mediump vec3 u_xlat16_11;
float u_xlat18;
mediump float u_xlat16_19;
float u_xlat27;
mediump float u_xlat16_29;
mediump float u_xlat16_32;
mediump float u_xlat16_34;
void main()
{
    u_xlat16_0.xy = texture(_MixMap, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy).xz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = u_xlat16_0.x + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_0.y * _Emissive;
    u_xlat16_10 = u_xlat16_10 * _EmisssionScale;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _Mask * u_xlat16_1.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_19 = u_xlat16_1.x + (-_Cutoff);
    SV_Target0.w = u_xlat16_1.x;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlatb0 = !!(u_xlat16_19<0.0);
#else
    u_xlatb0 = u_xlat16_19<0.0;
#endif
    if(u_xlatb0){discard;}
    u_xlat0.xyz = _MainLightPosition.www * _MainLightColor.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.x = _faceshadowScale * 0.400000006 + 1.0;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat16_1.x = min(max(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat16_1.x = clamp(u_xlat16_1.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat0.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xxx;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * _MainLightColor.www;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = min(u_xlat16_1.xzw, _MainLightColor.www);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = max(u_xlat16_1.xzw, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat16_3.x = vs_TEXCOORD3.w;
    u_xlat16_3.y = vs_TEXCOORD4.w;
    u_xlat16_3.z = vs_TEXCOORD5.w;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_3.xyz, u_xlat16_3.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = max(u_xlat0.x, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat9.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * u_xlat0.xxx + _MainLightPosition.xyz;
    u_xlat4.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat16_3.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat9.xyz, u_xlat9.xyz);
    u_xlat0.x = inversesqrt(u_xlat0.x);
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xxx * u_xlat9.xyz;
    u_xlat16_3 = texture(_BumpMapNr, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_3.xyz * vec3(2.0, 2.0, 2.0) + vec3(-1.0, -1.0, -1.0);
    u_xlat16_6.xyz = u_xlat16_5.yyy * vs_TEXCOORD5.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyw = u_xlat16_5.xxx * vs_TEXCOORD4.xyz + u_xlat16_6.xyz;
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = u_xlat16_5.zzz * vs_TEXCOORD3.xyz + u_xlat16_5.xyw;
    u_xlat16_29 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_29 = inversesqrt(u_xlat16_29);
    u_xlat16_5.xyz = vec3(u_xlat16_29) * u_xlat16_5.xyz;
    u_xlat0.x = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat0.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat0.x = min(max(u_xlat0.x, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat0.x = clamp(u_xlat0.x, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat9.x = (-u_xlat0.x) * u_xlat0.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_6 = texture(_MainTex, vs_TEXCOORD0.xy);
    u_xlat16_29 = u_xlat16_6.w * u_xlat16_6.w + _RoughNessOffset;
    u_xlat16_29 = max(u_xlat16_29, 0.0399999991);
    u_xlat16_29 = min(u_xlat16_29, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_32 = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_29;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat16_32;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x + u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat16_32 / u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat9.x = u_xlat16_32 * u_xlat16_32 + 1.0;
    u_xlat9.x = float(1.0) / u_xlat9.x;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat0.x;
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat16_29 * 0.25 + 0.25;
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat18;
    u_xlat0.x = min(u_xlat0.x, 100.0);
    u_xlat18 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, _MainLightPosition.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * u_xlat18;
    u_xlat18 = log2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 * _ShadowPow;
    u_xlat18 = exp2(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat18 = u_xlat18 + _ShadowOffset;
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat18 = min(max(u_xlat18, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat18 = clamp(u_xlat18, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_1.xzw * vec3(u_xlat18);
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = max(u_xlat16_1.xzw, vec3(_ShadowScale));
    u_xlat0.x = u_xlat0.x * 0.0399999991;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xxx * _SpecularColor.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xzw = u_xlat0.xzw * vec3(1.20000005, 1.20000005, 1.20000005);
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_2.xyz * u_xlat0.xzw;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = (-_colorSkin.xyz) + vec3(1.0, 1.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_3.www * u_xlat16_7.xyz + _colorSkin.xyz;
    u_xlat16_7.xyz = u_xlat16_6.xyz * u_xlat16_7.xyz;
    u_xlat16_1.xzw = u_xlat16_7.xyz * u_xlat16_1.xzw + u_xlat16_2.xyz;
    u_xlat16_2.x = dot((-u_xlat4.xyz), u_xlat16_5.xyz);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_2.x + u_xlat16_2.x;
    u_xlat16_2.xyz = u_xlat16_5.xyz * (-u_xlat16_2.xxx) + (-u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = dot(u_xlat16_5.xyz, u_xlat4.xyz);
    u_xlat16_32 = abs(u_xlat16_32) + 0.00400000019;
    u_xlat16_32 = min(u_xlat16_32, 1.0);
    u_xlat16_34 = (-u_xlat16_29) * 0.699999988 + 1.70000005;
    u_xlat16_34 = u_xlat16_29 * u_xlat16_34;
    u_xlat16_34 = u_xlat16_34 * 6.0;
    u_xlat16_3 = textureLod(unity_SpecCube0, u_xlat16_2.xyz, u_xlat16_34);
    u_xlat16_2.x = u_xlat16_3.w + -1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = unity_SpecCube0_HDR.w * u_xlat16_2.x + 1.0;
    u_xlat16_2.x = max(u_xlat16_2.x, 0.0);
    u_xlat16_2.x = log2(u_xlat16_2.x);

    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
    gl_Position.xyw = u_xlat0.xyw;
    return;
}

float u_xlat6;
void main()
{
    vs_TEXCOORD0.xy = in_TEXCOORD0.xy * _BaseMap_ST.xy + _BaseMap_ST.zw;
    u_xlat0.xyz = in_POSITION0.yyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[1].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[0].xyz * in_POSITION0.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[2].xyz * in_POSITION0.zzz + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat0.xyz + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_ObjectToWorld[3].xyz;
    u_xlat0.xyz = _LightDirection.xyz * _ShadowBias.xxx + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1.x = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[0].xyz);
    u_xlat1.y = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[1].xyz);
    u_xlat1.z = dot(in_NORMAL0.xyz, hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_WorldToObject[2].xyz);
    u_xlat6 = dot(u_xlat1.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
    u_xlat6 = max(u_xlat6, 1.17549435e-38);
    u_xlat6 = inversesqrt(u_xlat6);
    u_xlat1.xyz = vec3(u_xlat6) * u_xlat1.xyz;
    u_xlat6 = dot(_LightDirection.xyz, u_xlat1.xyz);
#ifdef UNITY_ADRENO_ES3
    u_xlat6 = min(max(u_xlat6, 0.0), 1.0);
#else
    u_xlat6 = clamp(u_xlat6, 0.0, 1.0);
#endif
    u_xlat6 = (-u_xlat6) + 1.0;
    u_xlat6 = u_xlat6 * _ShadowBias.y;
    u_xlat0.xyz = u_xlat1.xyz * vec3(u_xlat6) + u_xlat0.xyz;
    u_xlat1 = u_xlat0.yyyy * hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[1];
    u_xlat1 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[0] * u_xlat0.xxxx + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[2] * u_xlat0.zzzz + u_xlat1;
    u_xlat0 = u_xlat0 + hlslcc_mtx4x4unity_MatrixVP[3];
    gl_Position.z = max((-u_xlat0.w), u_xlat0.z);
